app/Dockerfile (dockerfile)
===========================
Tests: 20 (SUCCESSES: 19, FAILURES: 1)
Failures: 1 (HIGH: 1, CRITICAL: 0)

DS-0002 (HIGH): Specify at least 1 USER command in Dockerfile with non-root user as argument
════════════════════════════════════════
Running containers with 'root' user can lead to a container escape situation. It is a best practice to run containers as non-root users, which can be done by adding a 'USER' statement to the Dockerfile.

See https://avd.aquasec.com/misconfig/ds-0002

DS-0029 (HIGH): '--no-install-recommends' flag is missed: 'apt-get update -qq && DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive apt-get install -yq git wget libssl-dev build-essential  ninja-build python3 pkgconf libglib2.0-dev && apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/* /tmp/* /var/tmp/*'
════════════════════════════════════════

See https://avd.aquasec.com/misconfig/ds-0029
